    <a id="28945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28950" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#28845" class="Function">sucμ</a>
  <a id="28962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">—→⟨</a> <a id="28966" href="plfa.Lambda.html#19815" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="28972" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28973" href="plfa.Lambda.html#19815" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="28979" href="plfa.Lambda.html#20343" class="InductiveConstructor">β-μ</a><a id="28982" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28984" href="plfa.Lambda.html#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="28990" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28995" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="29000" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="29005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#28845" class="Function">sucμ</a>
  <a id="29012" class="Comment">--  ...</a>
  <a id="29022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22507" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Since every Agda computation must terminate,
we cannot simply ask Agda to reduce a term to a value.
Instead, we will provide a natural number to Agda, and permit it
to stop short of a value if the term requires more than the given
number of reduction steps.

A similar issue arises with cryptocurrencies.  Systems which use
smart contracts require the miners that maintain the blockchain to
evaluate the program which embodies the contract.  For instance,
validating a transaction on Ethereum may require executing a program
for the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM).  A long-running or
non-terminating program might cause the miner to invest arbitrary
effort in validating a contract for little or no return.  To avoid
this situation, each transaction is accompanied by an amount of _gas_
available for computation.  Each step executed on the EVM is charged
an advertised amount of gas, and the transaction pays for the gas at a
published rate: a given number of Ethers (the currency of Ethereum)
per unit of gas.

By analogy, we will use the name _gas_ for the parameter which puts a
bound on the number of reduction steps.  `Gas` is specified by a natural number:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="30196" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Gas"></a><a id="30201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30201" class="Datatype">Gas</a> <a id="30205" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30207" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="30211" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Gas.gas"></a><a id="30219" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30219" class="InductiveConstructor">gas</a> <a id="30223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30225" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="30227" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30229" href="plfa.Properties.html#30201" class="Datatype">Gas</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}When our evaluator returns a term `N`, it will either give evidence that
`N` is a value or indicate that it ran out of gas:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="30365" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Finished"></a><a id="30370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30370" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="30379" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30380" href="plfa.Properties.html#30380" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="30382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30384" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3717" class="Datatype">Term</a><a id="30388" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30390" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30392" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="30396" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="Finished.done"></a><a id="30405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30405" class="InductiveConstructor">done</a> <a id="30410" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="30418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#11490" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="30424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30380" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="30432" class="Comment">----------</a>
    <a id="30447" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30370" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="30458" href="plfa.Properties.html#30380" class="Bound">N</a>

  <a id="Finished.out-of-gas"></a><a id="30463" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30463" class="InductiveConstructor">out-of-gas</a> <a id="30474" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="30482" class="Comment">----------</a>
      <a id="30499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30370" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="30508" href="plfa.Properties.html#30380" class="Bound">N</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Given a term `L` of type `A`, the evaluator will, for some `N`, return
a reduction sequence from `L` to `N` and an indication of whether
reduction finished:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="30675" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Steps"></a><a id="30680" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30680" class="Datatype">Steps</a> <a id="30686" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30687" href="plfa.Properties.html#30687" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="30689" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3717" class="Datatype">Term</a><a id="30695" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30697" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30699" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="30703" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="Steps.steps"></a><a id="30712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30712" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a> <a id="30718" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30720" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="30722" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30723" href="plfa.Properties.html#30723" class="Bound">N</a><a id="30724" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="30730" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30687" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="30734" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22474" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="30737" href="plfa.Properties.html#30723" class="Bound">N</a>
    <a id="30743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30745" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30370" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="30754" href="plfa.Properties.html#30723" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="30762" class="Comment">----------</a>
    <a id="30777" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30680" class="Datatype">Steps</a> <a id="30785" href="plfa.Properties.html#30687" class="Bound">L</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The evaluator takes gas and evidence that a term is well typed,
and returns the corresponding steps:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="eval"></a><a id="30896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30896" class="Function">eval</a> <a id="30901" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30903" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="30905" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30906" href="plfa.Properties.html#30906" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="30908" href="plfa.Properties.html#30908" class="Bound">A</a><a id="30909" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="30913" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30201" class="Datatype">Gas</a>
  <a id="30921" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#30983" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="30925" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="30927" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30906" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="30929" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="30931" href="plfa.Properties.html#30908" class="Bound">A</a>
    <a id="30937" class="Comment">---------</a>
  <a id="30949" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30680" class="Datatype">Steps</a> <a id="30957" href="plfa.Properties.html#30906" class="Bound">L</a>
<a id="30959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30896" class="Function">eval</a> <a id="30964" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30965" href="plfa.Properties.html#30965" class="Bound">L</a><a id="30966" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30968" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30969" href="plfa.Properties.html#30219" class="InductiveConstructor">gas</a> <a id="30973" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#183" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="30977" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="30982" href="plfa.Properties.html#30982" class="Bound">⊢L</a>                             <a id="31013" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="31016" href="plfa.Properties.html#30712" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a> <a id="31022" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31023" href="plfa.Properties.html#30965" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="31025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22507" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∎</a><a id="31026" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31028" href="plfa.Properties.html#30463" class="InductiveConstructor">out-of-gas</a>
<a id="31039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30896" class="Function">eval</a> <a id="31044" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31045" href="plfa.Properties.html#31045" class="Bound">L</a><a id="31046" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31049" href="plfa.Properties.html#30219" class="InductiveConstructor">gas</a> <a id="31053" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31054" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#196" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="31058" href="plfa.Properties.html#31058" class="Bound">m</a><a id="31059" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="31062" href="plfa.Properties.html#31062" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="31065" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="31070" href="plfa.Properties.html#7735" class="Function">progress</a> <a id="31079" href="plfa.Properties.html#31062" class="Bound">⊢L</a>
<a id="31082" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="31086" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="31088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#7443" class="InductiveConstructor">done</a> <a id="31093" href="plfa.Properties.html#31093" class="Bound">VL</a>                                         <a id="31136" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="31139" href="plfa.Properties.html#30712" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a> <a id="31145" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31146" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="31148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22507" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∎</a><a id="31149" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31151" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31152" href="plfa.Properties.html#30405" class="InductiveConstructor">done</a> <a id="31157" href="plfa.Properties.html#31093" class="Bound">VL</a><a id="31159" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="31161" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="31165" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="31167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#7380" class="InductiveConstructor">step</a> <a id="31172" href="plfa.Properties.html#31172" class="Bound">L—→M</a> <a id="31177" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="31182" href="plfa.Properties.html#30896" class="Function">eval</a> <a id="31187" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31188" href="plfa.Properties.html#30219" class="InductiveConstructor">gas</a> <a id="31192" class="Bound">m</a><a id="31193" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31195" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31196" href="plfa.Properties.html#26610" class="Function">preserve</a> <a id="31205" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="31208" href="plfa.Properties.html#31172" class="Bound">L—→M</a><a id="31212" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="31214" class="Symbol">...</a>    <a id="31221" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="31223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30712" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a> <a id="31229" href="plfa.Properties.html#31229" class="Bound">M—↠N</a> <a id="31234" href="plfa.Properties.html#31234" class="Bound">fin</a>                               <a id="31268" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="31271" href="plfa.Properties.html#30712" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a> <a id="31277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31278" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="31280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">—→⟨</a> <a id="31284" class="Bound">L—→M</a> <a id="31289" href="plfa.Lambda.html#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="31291" href="plfa.Properties.html#31229" class="Bound">M—↠N</a><a id="31295" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31297" href="plfa.Properties.html#31234" class="Bound">fin</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Let `L` be the name of the term we are reducing, and `⊢L` be the
evidence that `L` is well typed.  We consider the amount of gas
remaining.  There are two possibilities:

* It is zero, so we stop early.  We return the trivial reduction
  sequence `L —↠ L`, evidence that `L` is well typed, and an
  indication that we are out of gas.

* It is non-zero and after the next step we have `m` gas remaining.
  Apply progress to the evidence that term `L` is well typed.  There
  are two possibilities:

  + Term `L` is a value, so we are done. We return the
    trivial reduction sequence `L —↠ L`, evidence that `L` is
    well-typed, and the evidence that `L` is a value.

  + Term `L` steps to another term `M`.  Preservation provides
    evidence that `M` is also well typed, and we recursively invoke
    `eval` on the remaining gas.  The result is evidence that
    `M —↠ N`, together with evidence that `N` is well typed and an
    indication of whether reduction finished.  We combine the evidence
    that `L —→ M` and `M —↠ N` to return evidence that `L —↠ N`,
    together with the other relevant evidence.


### Examples

We can now use Agda to compute the non-terminating reduction
sequence given earlier.  First, we show that the term `sucμ`
is well typed:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊢sucμ"></a><a id="32575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#32575" class="Function">⊢sucμ</a> <a id="32581" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#30983" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="32585" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="32587" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="32589" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a> <a id="32593" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="32595" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32600" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3736" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="32602" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a> <a id="32606" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="32608" href="plfa.Lambda.html#29349" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>
<a id="32611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#32575" class="Function">⊢sucμ</a> <a id="32617" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="32619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#34028" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢μ</a> <a id="32622" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32623" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33768" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢suc</a> <a id="32628" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32629" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33404" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢`</a> <a id="32632" href="plfa.Properties.html#32647" class="Function">∋x</a><a id="32634" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="32639" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="32647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#32647" class="Function">∋x</a> <a id="32650" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="32652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#32227" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}To show the first three steps of the infinite reduction
sequence, we evaluate with three steps worth of gas:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="32771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#32771" class="Function">_</a> <a id="32773" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32775" href="plfa.Properties.html#30896" class="Function">eval</a> <a id="32780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32781" href="plfa.Properties.html#30219" class="InductiveConstructor">gas</a> <a id="32785" class="Number">3</a><a id="32786" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32788" href="plfa.Properties.html#32575" class="Function">⊢sucμ</a> <a id="32794" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a>
  <a id="32798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30712" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a>
   <a id="32807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="32810" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a> <a id="32814" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="32816" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32821" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3736" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="32823" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a>
   <a id="32830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">—→⟨</a> <a id="32834" href="plfa.Lambda.html#20343" class="InductiveConstructor">β-μ</a> <a id="32838" href="plfa.Lambda.html#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="32844" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32849" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32850" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="32852" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a> <a id="32856" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="32858" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32863" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3736" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="32865" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a><a id="32868" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="32873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">—→⟨</a> <a id="32877" href="plfa.Lambda.html#19815" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="32883" href="plfa.Lambda.html#20343" class="InductiveConstructor">β-μ</a> <a id="32887" href="plfa.Lambda.html#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="32893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32898" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32899" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32905" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="32907" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a> <a id="32911" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="32913" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32918" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3736" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="32920" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a><a id="32923" class="Symbol">))</a>
   <a id="32929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">—→⟨</a> <a id="32933" href="plfa.Lambda.html#19815" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="32939" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32940" href="plfa.Lambda.html#19815" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="32946" href="plfa.Lambda.html#20343" class="InductiveConstructor">β-μ</a><a id="32949" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32951" href="plfa.Lambda.html#22548" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="32957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32962" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32963" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32968" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32969" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32975" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="32977" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a> <a id="32981" href="plfa.Lambda.html#4004" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="32983" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3903" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="32988" href="plfa.Lambda.html#3736" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="32990" class="String">&quot;x&quot;</a><a id="32993" class="Symbol">)))</a>
   <a id="33000" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22507" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∎</a><a id="33001" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="33006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30463" class="InductiveConstructor">out-of-gas</a>
<a id="33017" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="33019" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33021" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Similarly, we can use Agda to compute the reductions sequences given
in the previous chapter.  We start with the Church numeral two
applied to successor and zero.  Supplying 100 steps of gas is more than enough:

   <a id="33687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22507" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∎</a><a id="33688" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="33693" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30405" class="InductiveConstructor">done</a> <a id="33699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#11627" class="InductiveConstructor">V-suc</a> <a id="33706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33707" href="plfa.Lambda.html#11627" class="InductiveConstructor">V-suc</a> <a id="33713" href="plfa.Lambda.html#11579" class="InductiveConstructor">V-zero</a><a id="33719" class="Symbol">)))</a>
<a id="33723" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="33725" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33727" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The example above was generated by using `C-c C-n` to normalise the
left-hand side of the equation and pasting in the result as the
right-hand side of the equation.  The example reduction of the
previous chapter was derived from this result, reformatting and
writing `twoᶜ` and `sucᶜ` in place of their expansions.

Next, we show two plus two is four:

<a id="37819" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="37821" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37823" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Again, the derivation in the previous chapter was derived by
editing the above.

Similarly, we can evaluate the corresponding term for Church numerals:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="37988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#37988" class="Function">_</a> <a id="37990" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37992" href="plfa.Properties.html#30896" class="Function">eval</a> <a id="37997" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37998" href="plfa.Properties.html#30219" class="InductiveConstructor">gas</a> <a id="38002" class="Number">100</a><a id="38005" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#39116" class="Function">⊢2+2ᶜ</a> <a id="38013" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a>
  <a id="38017" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#30712" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a>

above.

#### Exercise `subject_expansion`

We say that `M` _reduces_ to `N` if `M —→ N`,
but we can also describe the same situation by saying
that `N` _expands_ to `M`.
The preservation property is sometimes called _subject reduction_.
Its opposite is _subject expansion_, which holds if
`M —→ N` and `∅ ⊢ N ⦂ A` imply `∅ ⊢ M ⦂ A`.
Find two counter-examples to subject expansion, one
with case expressions and one not involving case expressions.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="41175" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

## Well-typed terms don't get stuck

A term is _normal_ if it cannot reduce:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="Normal"></a><a id="41285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41285" class="Function">Normal</a> <a id="41292" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3717" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="41299" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41301" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="41305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41285" class="Function">Normal</a> <a id="41312" href="plfa.Properties.html#41312" class="Bound">M</a>  <a id="41315" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="41318" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="41320" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41321" href="plfa.Properties.html#41321" class="Bound">N</a><a id="41322" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41324" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41326" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="41328" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41329" href="plfa.Properties.html#41312" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41331" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#19499" class="Datatype Operator">—→</a> <a id="41334" href="plfa.Properties.html#41321" class="Bound">N</a><a id="41335" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
A term is _stuck_ if it is normal yet not a value:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="Stuck"></a><a id="41397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41397" class="Function">Stuck</a> <a id="41403" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#3717" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="41410" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41412" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="41416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41397" class="Function">Stuck</a> <a id="41422" href="plfa.Properties.html#41422" class="Bound">M</a>  <a id="41425" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="41428" href="plfa.Properties.html#41285" class="Function">Normal</a> <a id="41435" href="plfa.Properties.html#41422" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41437" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="41439" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="41441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#11490" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="41447" href="plfa.Properties.html#41422" class="Bound">M</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Using progress, it is easy to show that no well-typed term is stuck:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="41527" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
  <a id="unstuck"></a><a id="41539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41539" class="Postulate">unstuck</a> <a id="41547" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41549" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="41551" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41552" href="plfa.Properties.html#41552" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41554" href="plfa.Properties.html#41554" class="Bound">A</a><a id="41555" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="41561" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41563" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#30983" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="41565" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="41567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41552" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41569" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="41571" href="plfa.Properties.html#41554" class="Bound">A</a>
      <a id="41579" class="Comment">-----------</a>
    <a id="41595" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41597" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="41599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41397" class="Function">Stuck</a> <a id="41606" href="plfa.Properties.html#41552" class="Bound">M</a><a id="41607" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Using preservation, it is easy to show that after any number of steps,
a well-typed term remains well typed:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="41727" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
  <a id="preserves"></a><a id="41739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41739" class="Postulate">preserves</a> <a id="41749" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41751" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="41753" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41754" href="plfa.Properties.html#41754" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41756" href="plfa.Properties.html#41756" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="41758" href="plfa.Properties.html#41758" class="Bound">A</a><a id="41759" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="41765" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#30983" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="41769" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="41771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41754" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41773" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="41775" href="plfa.Properties.html#41758" class="Bound">A</a>
    <a id="41781" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41754" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22474" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="41788" href="plfa.Properties.html#41756" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="41796" class="Comment">---------</a>
    <a id="41810" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41812" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#30983" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="41814" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="41816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41756" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="41818" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="41820" href="plfa.Properties.html#41758" class="Bound">A</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
An easy consequence is that starting from a well-typed term, taking
any number of reduction steps leads to a term that is not stuck:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="41964" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
  <a id="wttdgs"></a><a id="41976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41976" class="Postulate">wttdgs</a> <a id="41983" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41985" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="41987" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41988" href="plfa.Properties.html#41988" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="41990" href="plfa.Properties.html#41990" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="41992" href="plfa.Properties.html#41992" class="Bound">A</a><a id="41993" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="41999" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#30983" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="42003" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="42005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41988" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="42007" href="plfa.Lambda.html#33348" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="42009" href="plfa.Properties.html#41992" class="Bound">A</a>
    <a id="42015" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42017" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41988" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="42019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#22474" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="42022" href="plfa.Properties.html#41990" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="42030" class="Comment">-----------</a>
    <a id="42046" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42048" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="42050" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="42051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#41397" class="Function">Stuck</a> <a id="42057" href="plfa.Properties.html#41990" class="Bound">N</a><a id="42058" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Felleisen and Wright, who introduced proofs via progress and
preservation, summarised this result with the slogan _well-typed terms
don't get stuck_.  (They were referring to earlier work by Robin
Milner, who used denotational rather than operational semantics. He
introduced `wrong` as the denotation of a term with a type error, and
showed _well-typed terms don't go wrong_.)

#### Exercise `stuck`

Give an example of an ill-typed term that does get stuck.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="42529" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
#### Exercise `unstuck` (recommended)

Provide proofs of the three postulates, `unstuck`, `preserves`, and `wttdgs` above.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="42685" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
## Reduction is deterministic

When we introduced reduction, we claimed it was deterministic.
For completeness, we present a formal proof here.

A case term takes four arguments (three subterms and a bound
variable), and our proof will need a variant
of congruence to deal with functions of four arguments.  It
is exactly analogous to `cong` and `cong₂` as defined previously:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="cong₄"></a><a id="43094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43094" class="Function">cong₄</a> <a id="43100" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43102" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="43104" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43105" href="plfa.Properties.html#43105" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="43107" href="plfa.Properties.html#43107" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="43109" href="plfa.Properties.html#43109" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="43111" href="plfa.Properties.html#43111" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="43113" href="plfa.Properties.html#43113" class="Bound">E</a> <a id="43115" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43117" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="43120" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="43123" href="plfa.Properties.html#43123" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="43125" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43127" href="plfa.Properties.html#43105" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="43129" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43131" href="plfa.Properties.html#43107" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="43133" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43135" href="plfa.Properties.html#43109" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="43137" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43139" href="plfa.Properties.html#43111" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="43141" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43143" href="plfa.Properties.html#43113" class="Bound">E</a><a id="43144" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="43148" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43149" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="43151" href="plfa.Properties.html#43151" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="43153" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43155" href="plfa.Properties.html#43105" class="Bound">A</a><a id="43156" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43158" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43159" href="plfa.Properties.html#43159" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="43161" href="plfa.Properties.html#43161" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="43163" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43165" href="plfa.Properties.html#43107" class="Bound">B</a><a id="43166" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43168" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43169" href="plfa.Properties.html#43169" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="43171" href="plfa.Properties.html#43171" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="43173" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43175" href="plfa.Properties.html#43109" class="Bound">C</a><a id="43176" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43178" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43179" href="plfa.Properties.html#43179" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="43181" href="plfa.Properties.html#43181" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="43183" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43185" href="plfa.Properties.html#43111" class="Bound">D</a><a id="43186" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="43190" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43149" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="43194" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="43196" href="plfa.Properties.html#43151" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="43198" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43200" href="plfa.Properties.html#43159" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="43202" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="43204" href="plfa.Properties.html#43161" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="43206" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43208" href="plfa.Properties.html#43169" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="43210" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="43212" href="plfa.Properties.html#43171" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="43214" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43216" href="plfa.Properties.html#43179" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="43218" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="43220" href="plfa.Properties.html#43181" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="43222" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43224" href="plfa.Properties.html#43123" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="43226" href="plfa.Properties.html#43149" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="43228" href="plfa.Properties.html#43159" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="43230" href="plfa.Properties.html#43169" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="43232" href="plfa.Properties.html#43179" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="43234" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="43236" href="plfa.Properties.html#43123" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="43238" href="plfa.Properties.html#43151" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="43240" href="plfa.Properties.html#43161" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="43242" href="plfa.Properties.html#43171" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="43244" href="plfa.Properties.html#43181" class="Bound">z</a>
<a id="43246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43094" class="Function">cong₄</a> <a id="43252" href="plfa.Properties.html#43252" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="43254" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="43259" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="43264" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="43269" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="43274" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="43276" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
It is now straightforward to show that reduction is deterministic:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="det"></a><a id="43357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43357" class="Function">det</a> <a id="43361" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43363" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="43365" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43366" href="plfa.Properties.html#43366" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="43368" href="plfa.Properties.html#43368" class="Bound">M′</a> <a id="43371" href="plfa.Properties.html#43371" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="43373" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="43391" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="43394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43366" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="43396" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#19499" class="Datatype Operator">—→</a> <a id="43399" href="plfa.Properties.html#43371" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="43401" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="43407" class="Comment">--------</a>
  <a id="43418" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43368" class="Bound">M′</a> <a id="43423" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="43425" href="plfa.Properties.html#43371" class="Bound">M″</a>

<a id="44444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43357" class="Function">det</a> <a id="44448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#20192" class="InductiveConstructor">β-suc</a> <a id="44455" href="plfa.Properties.html#44455" class="Bound">VL</a><a id="44457" class="Symbol">)</a>     <a id="44463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44464" href="plfa.Lambda.html#19898" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-case</a> <a id="44471" href="plfa.Properties.html#44471" class="Bound">L—→L″</a><a id="44476" class="Symbol">)</a>   <a id="44480" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="44483" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#294" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="44490" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44491" href="plfa.Properties.html#3503" class="Function">V¬—→</a> <a id="44496" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44497" href="plfa.Lambda.html#11627" class="InductiveConstructor">V-suc</a> <a id="44503" href="plfa.Properties.html#44455" class="Bound">VL</a><a id="44505" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44507" href="plfa.Properties.html#44471" class="Bound">L—→L″</a><a id="44512" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="44514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43357" class="Function">det</a> <a id="44518" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44519" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#20192" class="InductiveConstructor">β-suc</a> <a id="44525" class="Symbol">_)</a>      <a id="44533" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44534" href="plfa.Lambda.html#20192" class="InductiveConstructor">β-suc</a> <a id="44540" class="Symbol">_)</a>        <a id="44550" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="44553" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
<a id="44558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Properties.md %}{% raw %}#43357" class="Function">det</a> <a id="44562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md %}{% raw %}#20343" class="InductiveConstructor">β-μ</a>            <a id="44577" href="plfa.Lambda.html#20343" class="InductiveConstructor">β-μ</a>              <a id="44594" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="44597" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The proof is by induction over possible reductions.  We consider
three typical cases:

* Two instances of `ξ-·₁`:

      L —→ L′                 L —→ L″
      --------------- ξ-·₁    --------------- ξ-·₁
      L · M —→ L′ · M         L · M —→ L″ · M

  By induction we have `L′ ≡ L″`, and hence by congruence
  `L′ · M ≡ L″ · M`.

* An instance of `ξ-·₁` and an instance of `ξ-·₂`:

                              Value L
      L —→ L′                 M —→ M″
      --------------- ξ-·₁    --------------- ξ-·₂
      L · M —→ L′ · M         L · M —→ L · M″

  The rule on the left requires `L` to reduce, but the rule on the right
  requires `L` to be a value.  This is a contradiction since values do
  not reduce.  If the value constraint was removed from `ξ-·₂`, or from
  one of the other reduction rules, then determinism would no longer hold.

* Two instances of `β-ƛ`:

      Value V                              Value V
      ----------------------------- β-ƛ    ----------------------------- β-ƛ
      (ƛ x ⇒ N) · V —→ N [ x := V ]        (ƛ x ⇒ N) · V —→ N [ x := V ]

  Since the left-hand sides are identical, the right-hand sides are
  also identical. The formal proof simply invokes `refl`.

Five of the 18 lines in the above proof are redundant, e.g., the case
when one rule is `ξ-·₁` and the other is `ξ-·₂` is considered twice,
once with `ξ-·₁` first and `ξ-·₂` second, and the other time with the
two swapped.  What we might like to do is delete the redundant lines
and add

    det M—→M′ M—→M″ = sym (det M—→M″ M—→M′)

to the bottom of the proof. But this does not work: the termination
checker complains, because the arguments have merely switched order
and neither is smaller.


#### Quiz

Suppose we add a new term `zap` with the following reduction rule

    -------- β-zap
    M —→ zap

and the following typing rule:

    ----------- ⊢zap
    Γ ⊢ zap ⦂ A

Which of the following properties remain true in
the presence of these rules?  For each property, write either
"remains true" or "becomes false." If a property becomes
false, give a counterexample:

  - Determinism of `step`

  - Progress

  - Preservation


#### Quiz

Suppose instead that we add a new term `foo` with the following
reduction rules:

    ------------------ β-foo₁
    (λ x ⇒ ` x) —→ foo

    ----------- β-foo₂
    foo —→ zero

Which of the following properties remain true in
the presence of this rule?  For each one, write either
"remains true" or else "becomes false." If a property becomes
false, give a counterexample:

  - Determinism of `step`

  - Progress

  - Preservation


#### Quiz

Suppose instead that we remove the rule `ξ·₁` from the step
relation. Which of the following properties remain
true in the absence of this rule?  For each one, write either
"remains true" or else "becomes false." If a property becomes
false, give a counterexample:

  - Determinism of `step`

  - Progress

  - Preservation


#### Quiz

We can enumerate all the computable function from naturals to
naturals, by writing out all programs of type `` `ℕ ⇒ `ℕ`` in
lexical order.  Write `fᵢ` for the `i`'th function in this list.

Say we add a typing rule that applies the above enumeration
to interpret a natural as a function from naturals to naturals:

    Γ ⊢ L ⦂ `ℕ
    Γ ⊢ M ⦂ `ℕ
    -------------- _·ℕ_
    Γ ⊢ L · M ⦂ `ℕ

And that we add the corresponding reduction rule:

    fᵢ(m) —→ n
    ---------- δ
    i · m —→ n

Which of the following properties remain true in
the presence of this rule?  For each one, write either
"remains true" or else "becomes false." If a property becomes
false, give a counterexample:

  - Determinism of `step`

  - Progress

  - Preservation

Are all properties preserved in this case? Are there any
other alterations we would wish to make to the system?

## Unicode

This chapter uses the following unicode:

    ƛ  U+019B  LATIN SMALL LETTER LAMBDA WITH STROKE (\Gl-)
    Δ  U+0394  GREEK CAPITAL LETTER DELTA (\GD or \Delta)
    β  U+03B2  GREEK SMALL LETTER BETA (\Gb or \beta)
    δ  U+03B4  GREEK SMALL LETTER DELTA (\Gd or \delta)
    μ  U+03BC  GREEK SMALL LETTER MU (\Gm or \mu)
    ξ  U+03BE  GREEK SMALL LETTER XI (\Gx or \xi)
    ρ  U+03B4  GREEK SMALL LETTER RHO (\Gr or \rho)
    ᵢ  U+1D62  LATIN SUBSCRIPT SMALL LETTER I (\_i)
    ᶜ  U+1D9C  MODIFIER LETTER SMALL C (\^c)
    –  U+2013  EM DASH (\em)
    ₄  U+2084  SUBSCRIPT FOUR (\_4)
    ↠  U+21A0  RIGHTWARDS TWO HEADED ARROW (\rr-)
    ⇒  U+21D2  RIGHTWARDS DOUBLE ARROW (\=>)
    ∅  U+2205  EMPTY SET (\0)
    ∋  U+220B  CONTAINS AS MEMBER (\ni)
    ≟  U+225F  QUESTIONED EQUAL TO (\?=)
    ⊢  U+22A2  RIGHT TACK (\vdash or \|-)
    ⦂  U+2982  Z NOTATION TYPE COLON (\:)
